# In the rework, all focuses will be in one document. We will only use shared focuses, to make moving and redesigning trees easier

# Focus filters to use (note: focus filters should also be used for maluses. Minor effects for flavour purposes should not be marked): 
# FOCUS_FILTER_INTERNAL_AFFAIRS - story events
# FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY - industry (factories, output bonuses, consumer goods, resources)
# FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL - political power
# FOCUS_FILTER_STABILITY - stability
# FOCUS_FILTER_WAR_SUPPORT - war support
# FOCUS_FILTER_ARMY_BONUS - anything that adds to the army
# FOCUS_FILTER_AIRFORCE_BONUS - anything that adds to the airforce
# FOCUS_FILTER_NAVY_BONUS - anything that adds to the navy
# FOCUS_FILTER_MANPOWER - ponypower (not monthly population thought, too small of an effect)
# FOCUS_FILTER_RESEARCH - research slots, research speed bonuses, one-time bonuses for specific research
# FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION - any wargoals/wars
# Please add appropriate filters when creating a focus. Do not add any additional filters, it will break the UI. If in doubt, ping me in Project Heartlands. Thank you! - HerrB

# To make future understanding of the code easier, when referencing a state id, please comment the state name for clarity. Thank you! - HerrB

# Initial tree for Bronzehill, containing the starting industrial, military and policial trees. The focus tree will get expanded once the regency is declared
focus_tree = {
	id = bronzehill_initial_tree
	
	country = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 10
			tag = BRZ
			NOT = { has_country_flag = BRZ_revenge_tree_loaded }
		}
	}

	continuous_focus_position = { x = 0 y = 2500 }
	
	shared_focus = BRZ_finish_the_grover_v_industrial_park
	shared_focus = BRZ_military_budget_review
	shared_focus = BRZ_call_the_bronzehill_council
}

# Dawnclaw revenge tree
focus_tree = {
	id = bronzehill_revenge_tree
	
	country = { 
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 25
			tag = BRZ
			has_country_flag = BRZ_revenge_tree_loaded
		}
	}
	
	shared_focus = BRZ_the_catastrophy
	shared_focus = BRZ_finish_the_grover_v_industrial_park
	shared_focus = BRZ_military_budget_review
	shared_focus = BRZ_empire_of_dogs

	default = no

	continuous_focus_position = { x = 0 y = 2500 }
}

# Initial Industrial Tree
shared_focus = {
	id = BRZ_finish_the_grover_v_industrial_park
	icon = GFX_goal_generic_construct_civ_factory
	
	x = 5
	y = 0
	
	cost = 4
	
	ai_will_do = { factor = 10 }
	
	available = {
	}
	
	bypass = {
	}
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[Root.GetName]: Focus BRZ_finish_the_grover_v_industrial_park"#Auto-logging
		
		add_offsite_building = {
			type = industrial_complex
			level = 1
		}
		424 = { # Ravensburg
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = dam
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
				province = 10042
			}
		}
		
		country_event = bronzehill_industrial.1
	}
	
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY FOCUS_FILTER_INTERNAL_AFFAIRS }
}

shared_focus = {
	id = BRZ_paving_the_roads
	icon = GFX_infrastructure_road
	
	x = -1
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = BRZ_finish_the_grover_v_industrial_park
	
	cost = 3
	
	ai_will_do = { factor = 10 }
	
	prerequisite = {
		focus = BRZ_finish_the_grover_v_industrial_park
	}
	
	available = {
	}
	
	bypass = {
	}
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[Root.GetName]: Focus BRZ_paving_the_roads"#Auto-logging
		
		424 = { # Ravensburg
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }
}

shared_focus = {
	id = BRZ_contracts_with_the_businessgriffs
	icon = GFX_goal_endless_money
	
	x = 1
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = BRZ_paving_the_roads
	
	cost = 4
	
	ai_will_do = { factor = 10 }
	
	
	prerequisite = {
		focus = BRZ_paving_the_roads
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = BRZ_invite_griffenheim_engineers
	}
	
	available = {
	}
	
	bypass = {
	}
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[Root.GetName]: Focus BRZ_contracts_with_the_businessgriffs"#Auto-logging
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = BRZ_imperial_industry
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRZ_imperial_industry
				add_idea = BRZ_imperial_industry_2
			}
		}
		
		492 = { # Bronzekreuz
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		
		country_event = bronzehill_industrial.2
	}
	
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY FOCUS_FILTER_INTERNAL_AFFAIRS }
}

# Main industrial branch / Autonomist side
shared_focus = {
	id = BRZ_nationalize_the_grover_v_industrial_park
	icon = GFX_goal_treaty_fails
	
	x = -3
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = BRZ_contracts_with_the_businessgriffs
	
	cost = 6
	
	ai_will_do = { factor = 5 }
	
	prerequisite = {
		focus = BRZ_contracts_with_the_businessgriffs
	}
	
	mutually_exclusive = {
		focus = BRZ_negotiations_with_kraehe_stahl
	}
	
	available = {
		has_completed_focus = BRZ_a_change_of_course
	}
	
	bypass = {
	}
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[Root.GetName]: Focus BRZ_nationalize_the_grover_v_industrial_park"#Auto-logging
		
		# Punishment for nationalizing major industry
		add_political_power = -50
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = -0.1
		}
		
		424 = { # Raven Lakes
			remove_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
			}
		}
		
		# We do it this way so that the player always get shown a helpful tooltip
		# In theory, by this focus the player should always have BRZ_imperial_industry_2 
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = BRZ_imperial_industry
			}
			remove_ideas = BRZ_imperial_industry
		} 
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = BRZ_imperial_industry_2
			}
			remove_ideas = BRZ_imperial_industry_2
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_idea = BRZ_gotthilf_von_hohenau }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = available_political_advisor
			show_ideas_tooltip = BRZ_tilo_shovelpaw
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = BRZ_gotthilf_von_hohenau
			}
			
			deactivate_advisor = BRZ_gotthilf_von_hohenau
			activate_advisor = BRZ_tilo_shovelpaw
		}
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = BRZ_gotthilf_retire_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			retire_character = BRZ_gotthilf_von_hohenau
		}
	}
	
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL FOCUS_FILTER_STABILITY }
}

# Main industrial branch / Shared

shared_focus = {
	id = BRZ_expand_the_rural_school_budget
	icon = GFX_goal_griffon_schools
	
	x = 3
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = BRZ_nationalize_the_grover_v_industrial_park

shared_focus = {
	id = BRZ_political_background_checks
	icon = GFX_goal_skull_treaty
	
	x = -2
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = BRZ_rebuild_the_imperial_bureaucracy
	
	cost = 3
	
	ai_will_do = { factor = 8 }
	
	prerequisite = {
		focus = BRZ_rebuild_the_imperial_bureaucracy
	}
	
	available = {
	}
	
	bypass = {
	}
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[Root.GetName]: Focus BRZ_political_background_checks"#Auto-logging
		
		if = { # This is the last of the three focuses
			limit = {
				has_idea = BRZ_overstretched_bureaucracy_2_only_pol
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRZ_overstretched_bureaucracy_2_only_pol
				add_idea = BRZ_overstretched_bureaucracy_3
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Clerk was done, so legal is left
			limit = {
				has_idea = BRZ_overstretched_bureaucracy_2_clerks
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRZ_overstretched_bureaucracy_2_clerks
				add_idea = BRZ_overstretched_bureaucracy_2_only_legal
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Legal was done, so clerk is left
			limit = {
				has_idea = BRZ_overstretched_bureaucracy_2_legal
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRZ_overstretched_bureaucracy_2_legal
				add_idea = BRZ_overstretched_bureaucracy_2_only_clerks
			}
		}
		else = { # This is the first of the three focuses
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRZ_overstretched_bureaucracy_2
				add_idea = BRZ_overstretched_bureaucracy_2_pol
			}
		}
	}
	
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }
}

shared_focus = {
	id = BRZ_the_regent_in_exile
	icon = GFX_goal_tripartite_pact
	
	x = -3
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = BRZ_old_loyalties
	
	cost = 5 # Strawberry should declare independece 28 days after Eros was declared regent, so this needs to be 5 (to be sure)
	
	ai_will_do = { factor = 10 }
	
	mutually_exclusive = {
		focus = BRZ_the_rightful_regent
	}
	
	prerequisite = {
		focus = BRZ_old_loyalties
	}
	
	available = {
		GRI = {
			has_completed_focus = GRI_eros
		}
	}
	
	bypass = {
	}
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[Root.GetName]: Focus BRZ_the_regent_in_exile"#Auto-logging
		
		add_political_power = 50	
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of = GRI
			}
			GRI = {
				end_puppet = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = GRI
			}
			leave_faction = yes
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				STW = {
					is_in_faction = yes
				}
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = STW
				}
			}
			STW = {
				country_event = generic.2
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = STW }
			}
			give_guarantee = STW
			give_military_access = STW
			STW = {
				give_guarantee = BRZ
				give_military_access = BRZ
			}
			clr_country_flag = herzland_diplomacy_blocked
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = befriend
				id = GRI
				value = -200
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = protect
				id = GRI
				value = -200
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = send_volunteers_desire
				id = GRI
				value = -200
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = support
				id = GRI
				value = -200
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = alliance
				id = GRI
				value = -200
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = antagonize
				id = GRI
				value = 200
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = befriend
				id = STW
				value = 200
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = protect
				id = STW
				value = 200
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = send_volunteers_desire
				id = STW
				value = 200
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = support
				id = STW
				value = 200
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = alliance
				id = STW
				value = 200
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = antagonize
				id = STW
				value = -200
			}
		}
		
		clr_country_flag = herzland_diplomacy_blocked
	}

shared_focus = {
	id = BRZ_hunt_the_count
	icon = GFX_BRZ_count_ignatious_focus
	
	x = 0
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = BRZ_purge_the_nobles
	
	cost = 6
	
	ai_will_do = { factor = 10 }
	
	prerequisite = {
		focus = BRZ_purge_the_nobles
	}
	
	available = {
	}
	
	bypass = {
	}
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[Root.GetName]: Focus BRZ_hunt_the_count"#Auto-logging
		
		add_political_power = 25
		
		add_stability = 0.05
		
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		
		if = { # First choice: Griffenheim
			limit = {
				country_exists = GRI
			}
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = BRZ_count_ignatius_bronzetail
				}
				BRZ_count_ignatius_bronzetail = {
					set_nationality = GRI
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				GRI = {
					country_event = bronzehill_autonomist.1
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Second choice: Strawberry
			limit = {
				country_exists = STW
			}
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = BRZ_count_ignatius_bronzetail
				}
				BRZ_count_ignatius_bronzetail = {
					set_nationality = STW
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				STW = {
					country_event = bronzehill_autonomist.1
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # Nowhere to flee - dead
			retire_character = BRZ_count_ignatius_bronzetail
		}
		
		add_country_leader_role = { # Barnaby becomes underground leader of the non-aligned
			character = BRZ_barnaby_bronzetail
			country_leader = {
				desc = BRZ_BARNABY_DESC
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = centrism
				traits = { young_count }
			}
			promote_leader = yes
		}
		
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = neutrality
			name = BRZ_neutrality_party_barnaby
			long_name = BRZ_neutrality_party_barnaby_long
		}
	}
	
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL FOCUS_FILTER_STABILITY }
}

	id = BRZ_march_on_griffenheim
	icon = GFX_goal_generic_attack_allies
	
	x = 3
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = BRZ_march_of_the_working_dog
	
	cost = 6
	
	ai_will_do = { 
		base = 10 
	}
	
	prerequisite = {
		focus = BRZ_principle_of_total_dedication
		focus = BRZ_march_of_the_working_dog
		focus = BRZ_our_cause_for_justice
		focus = BRZ_unleash_the_dogs_of_war
	}
	
	mutually_exclusive = { 
	}
	
	available = {
		has_army_manpower = { size > 49999 } # 50k
	}
	
	bypass = {
		382 = {
			is_owned_by = ROOT
		}
	}
	
	will_lead_to_war_with = GRD # tag alias for event_target:griffonian_empire	 
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[Root.GetName]: Focus BRZ_march_on_griffenheim"#Auto-logging
	
		add_manpower = 20000 # Some idiots
	
		add_state_claim = 382 # Griffenheim
		add_state_claim = 405
		add_state_claim = 397
		add_state_claim = 437 # Crona
		add_state_claim = 555

		create_wargoal = {
			type = take_state_focus
			target = 382.owner
			generator = { 382 }
		}
		#Don't give wargoal on same country twice
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					437 = { # Crona (connection to Griffenheim)
						owner = { 
							owns_state = 382 # Griffenheim
							NOT = { tag = ROOT } 
						} 
					} 
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = take_state_focus
				target = 437.owner
				generator = { 437 }
			}
		}
		
	}
	
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION }
}

shared_focus = {
	id = BRZ_road_to_rottendedam
	icon = GFX_goal_Attack_Feathasia_2
	
	x = -2
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = BRZ_ignatius_regency
	
	cost = 8
	
	ai_will_do = { # First fight war to their end
		factor = 10 
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
	
	prerequisite = {
		focus = BRZ_ignatius_regency
	}
	
	available = {
	}
	
	bypass = {
		NOT = { country_exists = STW }
		NOT = { country_exists = FEA }
		NOT = { country_exists = PYT }
	}
	
	will_lead_to_war_with = STW # Strawberry
	will_lead_to_war_with = FEA # Feathisia
	will_lead_to_war_with = PYT # Greifenmarschen
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[Root.GetName]: Focus BRZ_road_to_rottendedam"#Auto-logging
		
		# Give wargoal on Strawberry, Feathisia and Greifenmarschen - if not at war
		if = { # Strawberry
			limit = {
				STW = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = STW
			}
		} 
		STW = {
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
				}
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = { # Feathisia
			limit = {
				FEA = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = FEA
			}
		} 
		FEA = {
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
				}
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = { # Greifenmarschen
			limit = {
				PYT = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = PYT
			}
		} 
		PYT = {
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
				}
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION }
}

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[Root.GetName]: Focus BRZ_call_up_the_knights"#Auto-logging
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = BRZ_knightsubjungtion_tt
		
		HLQ = { add_to_ROOT_potential_cores = yes } # Hellquill
		LNS = { add_to_ROOT_potential_cores = yes } # Longsword
		LSM = { add_to_ROOT_potential_cores = yes } # Longsword military
		LSC = { add_to_ROOT_potential_cores = yes } # Longsword communists
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				HLQ = { # Hellquill
					exists = yes
					is_puppet = no
					OR = { # reformisten are evil
						has_government = neutrality
						has_government = democratic
					}
				}
			}
			HLQ = {
				country_event = bronzehill_knightsubjungation.1
			}
		} else = { # Wargoal
			if = {
				limit = {
					HLQ = {
						exists = yes
						NOT = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
						NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
					}
				}
				create_wargoal = {
					type = annex_everything
					target = HLQ
				}
			} 
			HLQ = {
				every_core_state = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
					}
					add_claim_by = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		
		if = { # Longsword
			limit = {
				LSM = { # Longsword military
					exists = yes
					is_puppet = no
					OR = {
						has_government = neutrality
						has_government = democratic
					}
				}
			}
			LSM = {
				country_event = bronzehill_knightsubjungation.1
			}
		} else = { # Wargoal
			if = {
				limit = {
					LSM = {
						exists = yes
						NOT = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
						NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
					}
				}
				create_wargoal = {
					type = annex_everything
					target = LSM
				}
			} 
			LSM = {
				every_core_state = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
						NOT = { is_core_of = HLQ }
					}
					add_claim_by = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		if = { # No negotiations with reformisten
			limit = {
				LNS = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = LNS
			}
		} 
		LNS = {
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
					NOT = { is_core_of = HLQ }
				}
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = { # No negotiations with communists
			limit = {
				LSC = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = LSC
			}
		} 
		LSC = {
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
					NOT = { is_core_of = HLQ }
				}
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				537 = { # Hellquill
					NOT = { is_owned_by = HLQ }
					NOT = { is_owned_by = LNS }
					NOT = { is_owned_by = LSM }
					NOT = { is_owned_by = LSC }
					NOT = { is_owned_by = ROOT }
				}
				NOT = {
					any_subject_country = {
						owns_state = 537
					}
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = HL1 # Owner of Hellquill
			}
		}
	}
	
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION }
}

		}

shared_focus = {
	id = BRZ_attack_strawberry
	icon = GFX_goal_Attack_Strawberry_2
	
	x = -3
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = BRZ_barnabys_regency
	
	cost = 6
	
	ai_will_do = { # First fight war to their end
		factor = 10 
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
	
	prerequisite = {
		focus = BRZ_barnabys_regency
	}
	
	available = {
	}
	
	bypass = {
		NOT = { country_exists = STW }
	}
	
	will_lead_to_war_with = STW # Strawberry
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[Root.GetName]: Focus BRZ_attack_strawberry"#Auto-logging
		
		# Give wargoal on Strawberry - if not at war
		if = { # Strawberry
			limit = {
				STW = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = STW
			}
		} 
		STW = {
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
				}
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION }
}

	id = BRZ_destroy_aquileia

	x = 0
	y = 1

	cost = 6
	
	ai_will_do = { # First fight war to their end
		factor = 10 
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			has_war = yes
		}

	will_lead_to_war_with = JFT # "

	will_lead_to_war_with = HEL # Adelhard

	will_lead_to_war_with = FLO # Flovena
	will_lead_to_war_with = JE1 # Aquila's owner (tag alias)

		VIN = { add_to_ROOT_potential_cores = yes } # "

				target = STW
			}

	will_lead_to_war_with = FEZ # Fezeria
	will_lead_to_war_with = TR1 # Skyfalls owner (tag alias)
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[Root.GetName]: Focus BRZ_end_the_western_debauchery"#Auto-logging
		
		# Can core Skyfall/Fezeria
		
		TRD = { add_to_ROOT_potential_cores = yes } # Skyfall
		FEZ = { add_to_ROOT_potential_cores = yes } # Fezaria
		
		# Give wargoal on Skyfall and Fezeria
		if = { # Skyfall
			limit = {
				TRD = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = TRD
			}
		} 
		TRD = {
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
				}
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = { # Fezeria
			limit = {
				FEZ = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = FEZ
			}
		} 
		FEZ = {
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
				}
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = { # Any other owner of Skyfall
			limit = {
				381 = { # Skyfall
					NOT = { is_owned_by = TRD }
					NOT = { is_owned_by = FEZ }
					NOT = { is_owned_by = ROOT }
				}
				NOT = { # No wargoals against subjects
					any_subject_country = {
						owns_state = 381
					}
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = TR1 # 381.owner (tag alias)
			}
		}
	}
	
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION }

shared_focus = {
	id = BRZ_end_the_republican_insult
	icon = GFX_goal_griffonian_republic
	
	x = 1
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = BRZ_cleanse_the_cities
	
	cost = 6
	
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 10
	}

	}

		focus = BRZ_redraw_provincial_lines
	}
	
	available = {
	}
	
	bypass = {
	}
	
	will_lead_to_war_with = FAT
	will_lead_to_war_with = FAW
	will_lead_to_war_with = FA1 # Cloudbury's owner (tag alias)
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[Root.GetName]: Focus BRZ_end_the_republican_insult"#Auto-logging
		
		# Can core Griff Repulic
		
		FAT = { add_to_ROOT_potential_cores = yes } # Fatass = Griff Republic
		FAW = { add_to_ROOT_potential_cores = yes } # Fatass Warlord = Griff Republic Militarist Coup
		
		# Give wargoal on Griff Republic - if not at war
		if = { # Griff Republic
			limit = {
				FAT = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = FAT
			}
		} 
		FAT = {
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
				}
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = { # Griff Republic Warlord
			limit = {
				FAW = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = FAW
			}
		} 
		FAW = {
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
				}
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = { # Whoever else owns Cloudbury
			limit = {
				485 = { # Cloudbury
					NOT = { is_owned_by = FAT }
					NOT = { is_owned_by = FAW }
					NOT = { is_owned_by = ROOT }
				}
				NOT = {
					any_subject_country = {
						owns_state = 485 # Cloudbury
					}
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = FA1 # 485.owner (tag alias)
			}
		}
	}
	
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION }
}

					NOT = { is_owned_by = BAN }
					NOT = { is_owned_by = LAK }

					}

				type = annex_everything
				target = BO1 # Onwer of Griffenstone
			}
		}
	}

		log = "[Root.GetName]: Focus BRZ_unity_in_spirit"#Auto-logging
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "La Resistance"
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_ideas = BRZ_loyal_party
				remove_ideas = BRZ_loyal_palace_lar
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRZ_total_control_mock_diff_lar
				add_idea = BRZ_total_control_lar
			}
		}
		else = {
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_ideas = BRZ_loyal_party
				remove_ideas = BRZ_loyal_palace_nolar
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRZ_total_control_mock_diff_nolar
				add_idea = BRZ_total_control_nolar
			}
		}
		
		country_event = bronzehill_steelpawpostcoronation.2
	}
	
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_STABILITY FOCUS_FILTER_INTERNAL_AFFAIRS }
}

shared_focus = {
	id = BRZ_liberate_strawberry_softfur
	icon = GFX_goal_Attack_Strawberry_2
	
	x = -3
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = BRZ_softfurs_regency
	
	cost = 6
	
	ai_will_do = { # First fight war to their end
		factor = 10 
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
	
	prerequisite = {
		focus = BRZ_softfurs_regency
	}
	
	available = {
	}
	
	bypass = {
		NOT = { country_exists = STW }
	}
	
	will_lead_to_war_with = STW # Strawberry
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[Root.GetName]: Focus BRZ_liberate_strawberry_softfur"#Auto-logging
		
		# Give wargoal on Strawberry - if not at war
		if = { # Strawberry
			limit = {
				STW = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = STW
			}
		} 
		STW = {
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
				}
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION }
}

shared_focus = {
	id = BRZ_reclaim_skyfall
	icon = GFX_goal_Attack_Skyfall
	
	x = 1
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = BRZ_integrate_the_agrarians
	
	cost = 6
	
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 10
	}
	
	prerequisite = {
		focus = BRZ_integrate_the_agrarians
		focus = BRZ_follow_the_cappoodle_doctrine
	}
	
	available = {
	}
	
	bypass = {
	}
	
	will_lead_to_war_with = TRD # Skyfall
	will_lead_to_war_with = FEZ # Fezeria
	will_lead_to_war_with = TR1 # Owner of Skyfall (tag alias)
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[Root.GetName]: Focus BRZ_reclaim_skyfall"#Auto-logging
		
		# Can core Skyfall/Fezeria
		
		TRD = { add_to_ROOT_potential_cores = yes } # Skyfall
		FEZ = { add_to_ROOT_potential_cores = yes } # Fezaria
		
		# Give wargoal on Skyfall and Fezeria
		if = { # Skyfall
			limit = {
				TRD = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = TRD
			}
		} 
		TRD = {
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
				}
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = { # Fezeria
			limit = {
				FEZ = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = FEZ
			}
		} 
		FEZ = {
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
				}
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = { # Any other owner of Skyfall
			limit = {
				381 = { # Skyfall
					NOT = { is_owned_by = TRD }
					NOT = { is_owned_by = FEZ }
					NOT = { is_owned_by = ROOT }
				}
				NOT = { # No wargoals against subjects
					any_subject_country = {
						owns_state = 381
					}
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = TR1 # 381.owner (tag alias)
			}
		}
	}
	
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION }
}

		}
	}

	}

	continue_if_invalid = no
	available_if_capitulated = no
	
	will_lead_to_war_with = STW # Strawberry
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[Root.GetName]: Focus BRZ_strawberrian_riches"#Auto-logging
		
		# Give wargoal on Strawberry - if not at war
		if = { # Strawberry
			limit = {
				STW = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = STW
			}
		} 
		STW = {
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
				}
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION }
}

		TRD = { add_to_ROOT_potential_cores = yes } # Skyfall
		FEZ = { add_to_ROOT_potential_cores = yes } # Fezaria
		
		# Give wargoal on Skyfall and Fezeria
		if = { # Skyfall
			limit = {
				TRD = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = TRD
			}
		} 
		TRD = {
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
				}
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = { # Fezeria
			limit = {
				FEZ = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = FEZ
			}
		} 
		FEZ = {
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
				}
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = { # Any other owner of Skyfall
			limit = {
				381 = { # Skyfall
					NOT = { is_owned_by = TRD }
					NOT = { is_owned_by = FEZ }
					NOT = { is_owned_by = ROOT }
				}
				NOT = { # No wargoals against subjects
					any_subject_country = {
						owns_state = 381
					}
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = TR1 # 381.owner (tag alias)
			}
		}
	}
	
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION }
}

shared_focus = {
	id = BRZ_call_up_the_knights_loudbark
	icon = GFX_goal_Griffonian_Heer_2
	
	x = 1
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = BRZ_the_veterans_land_act
	
	cost = 6
	
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 10
	}
	
	prerequisite = {
		focus = BRZ_the_veterans_land_act
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = BRZ_our_duties_to_the_peasantry
	}
	
	available = {
		has_global_flag = LNS_civil_war_end_flag
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = HLQ
			}
			HLQ = {
				has_war = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = LSC
			}
			LSC = {
				has_war = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = LSM
			}
			LSM = {
				has_war = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = LNS
			}
			LNS = {
				has_war = no
			}
		}
	}
	
	bypass = {
	}
	
	cancel_if_invalid = yes
	continue_if_invalid = no
	available_if_capitulated = no
	
	will_lead_to_war_with = HLQ # Hellquill
	will_lead_to_war_with = LNS # Longsword
	will_lead_to_war_with = LSM # Longsword Militarist
	will_lead_to_war_with = LSC # Longsword Communists
	will_lead_to_war_with = HL1 # Hellquill owner
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[Root.GetName]: Focus BRZ_call_up_the_knights_loudbark"#Auto-logging
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = BRZ_knightsubjungtion_tt
		
		HLQ = { add_to_ROOT_potential_cores = yes } # Hellquill
		LNS = { add_to_ROOT_potential_cores = yes } # Longsword
		LSM = { add_to_ROOT_potential_cores = yes } # Longsword military
		LSC = { add_to_ROOT_potential_cores = yes } # Longsword communists
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				HLQ = { # Hellquill
					exists = yes
					is_puppet = no
					OR = { # reformisten are evil
						has_government = neutrality
						has_government = democratic
					}
				}
			}
			HLQ = {
				country_event = bronzehill_knightsubjungation.1
			}
		} else = { # Wargoal
			if = {
				limit = {
					HLQ = {
						exists = yes
						NOT = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
						NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
					}
				}
				create_wargoal = {
					type = annex_everything
					target = HLQ
				}
			} 
			HLQ = {
				every_core_state = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
					}
					add_claim_by = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		
		if = { # Longsword
			limit = {
				LSM = { # Longsword military
					exists = yes
					is_puppet = no
					OR = {
						has_government = neutrality
						has_government = democratic
					}
				}
			}
			LSM = {
				country_event = bronzehill_knightsubjungation.1
			}
		} else = { # Wargoal
			if = {
				limit = {
					LSM = {
						exists = yes
						NOT = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
						NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
					}
				}
				create_wargoal = {
					type = annex_everything
					target = LSM
				}
			} 
			LSM = {
				every_core_state = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
						NOT = { is_core_of = HLQ }
					}
					add_claim_by = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		if = { # No negotiations with reformisten
			limit = {
				LNS = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = LNS
			}
		} 
		LNS = {
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
					NOT = { is_core_of = HLQ }
				}
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = { # No negotiations with communists
			limit = {
				LSC = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = LSC
			}
		} 
		LSC = {
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
					NOT = { is_core_of = HLQ }
				}
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				537 = { # Hellquill
					NOT = { is_owned_by = HLQ }
					NOT = { is_owned_by = LNS }
					NOT = { is_owned_by = LSM }
					NOT = { is_owned_by = LSC }
					NOT = { is_owned_by = ROOT }
				}
				NOT = {
					any_subject_country = {
						owns_state = 537
					}
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = HL1 # Owner of Hellquill
			}
		}
	}
	
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION }
}

	will_lead_to_war_with = BAN # Blackrock Bandits
	will_lead_to_war_with = BO1 # Owner of Griffonstone
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[Root.GetName]: Focus BRZ_retake_griffonstone"#Auto-logging
		
		# Can core Griffenstone stuff
		
		BOI = { add_to_ROOT_potential_cores = yes } # Griffenstone
		LAK = { add_to_ROOT_potential_cores = yes } # Rumare
		BAN = { add_to_ROOT_potential_cores = yes } # Blackrock
		
		# Give wargoal on Griffenstone sphere - if not at war
		if = { # Griffenstone
			limit = {
				BOI = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = BOI
			}
		} 
		BOI = {
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
				}
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = { # Rumare
			limit = {
				LAK = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = LAK
			}
		} 
		LAK = {
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
				}
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = { # Blackrock
			limit = {
				BAN = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = BAN
			}
		} 
		BAN = {
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
				}
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				389 = { # Griffonstone
					NOT = { is_owned_by = BOI }
					NOT = { is_owned_by = BAN }
					NOT = { is_owned_by = LAK }
					NOT = { is_owned_by = ROOT }
				}
				NOT = {
					any_subject_country = {
						owns_state = 389
					}
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = BO1 # Onwer of Griffenstone
			}
		}
	}

				}
			}
			else = {

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[Root.GetName]: Focus BRZ_unite_with_our_eastern_brothers"#Auto-logging
		
		# Can core DMT
		
		DMT = { add_to_ROOT_potential_cores = yes } # Diamond Mountain
		
		if = { # Diamond Mountain
			limit = {
				DMT = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = DMT
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				637 = { # Capital of Diamond Mountain
					NOT = { is_owned_by = ROOT }
					NOT = { is_owned_by = DMT }
				}
				NOT = {
					any_subject_country = {
						owns_state = 637
					}
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = { # 637 = Capital of Diamond Mountain
				type = take_state_focus
				target = DM1
				generator = { 637 }
			}
		}
		DMT = {
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
				}
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION }
}

shared_focus = {
	id = BRZ_war_on_the_maarspawn
	icon = GFX_goal_generic_major_war
	
	x = 1
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = BRZ_rally_the_griffon_population
	
	cost = 6
	
	ai_will_do = { 
		factor = 1 
		modifier = { # Not attacking before 1010
			date < 1010.01.01
			factor = 0
		}
		modifier = { # Either strong enough or wait until Herzschmerz (fires before 1011)
			OR = {
				date > 1011.01.01
				has_army_manpower = { size > 149999 } # 150k
			}
			factor = 20
		}
	}
	
	prerequisite = {
		focus = BRZ_by_any_means_nessicary
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = BRZ_rally_the_griffon_population
	}
	
	available = { # Player requirements relaxed
		has_army_manpower = { size > 49999 } # 50k
		OR = {
			has_army_manpower = { size > 99999 } # 100k
			date > 1010.01.01
		}
	}
	
	bypass = {
		owns_state = 382 # Griffenheim
	}
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[Root.GetName]: Focus BRZ_war_on_the_maarspawn"#Auto-logging
		
		add_ideas = BRZ_death_to_the_traitors # attack bonus
	
		add_state_claim = 382 # Griffenheim
		add_state_claim = 405
		add_state_claim = 397
		add_state_claim = 437 # Crona
		add_state_claim = 555

		create_wargoal = {
			type = take_state_focus
			target = 382.owner
			generator = { 382 }
		}
		#Don't give wargoal on same country twice
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					437 = { # Crona (connection to Griffenheim)
						owner = { 
							owns_state = 382 # Griffenheim
							NOT = { tag = ROOT } 
						} 
					} 
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = take_state_focus
				target = 437.owner
				generator = { 437 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION }
}
